20.1(1): long mnyam pa nyid: sor rtogs bya grub ye shes lnga: zhing dang gzhal yas 'od zer 
20.2(1): dang : rgyan dang gdan khri yon tan lnga: bden gnyis dbyer med bdag nyid can:
20.3(1): 'og min gnas kyi mtha' 'das pa: gzhi ma gdul bya'i zhing kyang med: rang byung 
20.4(1): ye shes rang rtsal che: thig le gcig zlum zur bzhi rgyas: rang grub 'byung ba'i 
20.5(1): 'khor lo brtsegs: yon tan thams cad lhun gyis grub: dgos 'dod 'byung ba 
20.6(1): rin chen lnga: ye shes gzhal yas tshad la 'das: phyogs bcu yongs su rgya ma chad:
20.7(1): che ba'i yon tan dpag tu med: gdul bya mtshon phyir gru bzhi'i dbyibs: don 
20.8(1): rtags rang byung ye shes bzhi: rin chen lnga yi glo 'bur mdzes: dus gsum rgyal 
20.9(1): ba'i zhing kun khyab: rang bzhin mtshan nyid tha dad med: rang byung thig le nyag ma 
20.10(1): gcig: gzhal yas bum pa gcig tu zlum: ye shes bye brag bsam mi khyab: 'dod 
20.11(1): bskang brda' thabs sna tshogs gsal: 'od mdzes sgeg pa'i mchod sprin 'thor:
20.12(1): rnam par thar pa'i sgo bzhi ldan: phyi nang ma sgrib zang thal che: rin chen khri rkang 
20.13(1): rgyas pa'i steng : mi 'jigs stobs ldan lngas khri mdzes: pad+ma nyi ma zla ba'i steng :
20.14(1): ston pa kun tu bzang po nyid: zhabs phyag mnyam bzhag skyil mo krung : phyogs kun 
20.15(1): zhal ni thal ler gzigs: 'khor 'das mnyam nyid rol pa'i klong : rang byung sku 
20.16(1): dang zhing khams bdag: gnas pa'i 'khor dang ma spyad 'khor: snang stong 'dus ma 
20.17(1): byas pa'i sku: shes bya ma spyad kun bzang mo: klong las mi 'da' kun bzang mo:
20.18(1): thabs shes rol pa dbyer mi phyed: ngo bo klong las mi 'da' ste: snang ba'i rang 
20.19(1): bzhin mtshan ma med: rnam par sku dang ye shes shar: mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lo che:
20.20(1): phung khams skye mched lha lha mo: longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku dang zhing : bder 
20.21(1): gshegs rgyal ba kun 'dus skus: gti mug can dang tshangs pa klu: rnam par 
21.1(1): 'dul bar snang ba dang : g.yung drung gsal ba rang byung skus: zhe sdang can dang 
21.2(1): gnod sbyin 'dul: 'khor lo dge lha gar phyug skus: phrag dog can dang gyi ling 
21.3(1): 'dul: pad+ma bye brag dngos med skus: 'dod chags can dang mkha' 'gro 'dul:
21.4(1): rin chen dga' ba don grub skus: nga rgyal can dang gtogs 'dod 'dul: 'di 
21.5(1): bzhi'i theg pa bzhi po yis: gdul bya dam rdzas so so ru: snang ba zhen pa rnam bzhi 
21.6(1): la: rgyu 'bras zhen pa'i theg bzhis bstan: sangs rgyas sems can bzang ngan 
21.7(1): 'dzin: mos pa'i zhen pa grol ba'i phyir: mnyam pa bzhi dang lnga ru bstan: don mi 
21.8(1): mnyam yang tshig mnyam pa: skad du bstan pa'i theg pa bstan: lha mi nyan rang byang 
21.9(1): chub sems: 'dul phyir bzang ngan gsang sgor drang : thams cad blang dor med 
21.10(1): pa bstan: yun ring dka' spyad de dag gis: 'grub par dka' sems sgyid log 
21.11(1): na: mos pa tsam gyis 'grub pa'i don: bsnyen sgrub yan lag bzhi nyid la: bya ba 
21.12(1): du ma tshang ba dang : rgya che gsang sngags bslab par bya: lta ba dam tshig ting nge 
21.13(1): 'dzin: spyod pa mos la 'tsham pa bstan: gdul ba gsang ba sngags chen po: lta 
21.14(1): spyod skrag cing tshig chad sngangs: rang lta mngon zhen mi 'jug rnams: drang phyir 
21.15(1): nges pa'i don la gzhug: gdul bya mos pa gang mos pa: gzhan dbang rang snang skye 
21.16(1): ba med: mtshan nyid gsum gyis mthun drang phyir: thams cad don bsdus rang 
21.17(1): bzhin te: kun btags gzugs sogs yul drug dang : dbang po drug dag bon 
21.18(1): gang zag: dngos po yod do snyam du 'khrul: rnam shes nan gyis btags pa yis:
21.19(1): gzung 'dzin cha gnyis rtog pa de: kun gzhi'i rnam shes 'khor bcas nyid: rgyu 
21.20(1): 'bras tshul du skad cig ma: sems dang sems byung rten 'brel 'byung : gzhan 
21.21(1): dbang khams gsum sems can gyi: shes pa rgyu rkyen rag ma lus: rang skye mi nus 
22.1(1): gzhan dbang ste: rgyu rkyen bzhis bskyed de dang 'brel: kun gzhi bag chags rgyu yi 
22.2(1): rkyen: mig dbang tshogs drug bdag po'i rkyen: yul gzugs sgra sogs dmigs 
22.3(1): pa'i rkyen: shes pa skad cig ma 'gag pas: de ma thag pa'i rkyen gyis dbye: yongs 
22.4(1): grub gzhan dbang bon can kun: gzung 'dzin dang bral ba: de la yongs grub 
22.5(1): ces kyang bya: chu dang nam mkha' gser lta bu: rang bzhin ma 'ong gang ma song :
22.6(1): de bzhin bon nyid bon gyi dbyings: sangs rgyas 'jig rten du bstan kyang : gang 
22.7(1): nas ma 'ong ma bstan kyang : gang du ma song gang la bstan: med pa kun btags 
22.8(1): mtshan ma gsum: kun btags kun tu sgro btags pa: gzung 'dzin bon kun 
22.9(1): nan gyis btags: de ni kun btags mtshan nyid de: med pa kun btags la 
22.10(1): gnyis te: snang ba'i kun btags gzung 'dzin gnyis: mi snang kun btags ri 
22.11(1): bong rwa: mo gsham mu stegs bdag tu lta: nyan thos kyi ni rdul phran te: de la 
22.12(1): brgal te de gnyis kyang : gzhi med snang ba'i kun btags dang : mi snang ba yi 
22.13(1): kun btags gnyis: rgyu 'bras bon can ltos na snang : de la bskyed pa'i rgyu thob 
22.14(1): yod: bon rnams rang bzhin med pa ru: bon nyid rtogs na 'phags lam bskyed:
22.15(1): de nyid rtogs pa mthar phyin na: sku dang ye shes 'bras thob bstan: yod 'dod 
22.16(1): gzhan dbang mtshan nyid ni: gzhan gyi rkyen la rag las shing : rang mi 'byung bas 
22.17(1): rten 'brel 'byung : gzhan dbang mtshan nyid ces su bstan: mi 'gog gzhan 
22.18(1): dbang la yang gnyis: bskyed pa'i gzhan dbang ltos pa'i gzhan: sems las kun 
22.19(1): 'byung rkyen bskyed pas: deltos rgyu rkyen 'dus ma byas: so sor brtags dang 
22.20(1): brtag min 'gog: nam mkha' dang ni de bzhin nyid: brtags la yongs su sgrub 
22.21(1): pa ni: de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i: ye shes gnyis ni mi 'gyur ba: phyin ci 
23.1(1): ma log yongs rdzogs shing : grub pas yongs grub mtshan nyid de: yongs su grub 
23.2(1): la rnam pa gnyis: mi 'gyur ba yi yongs grub ni: bon rnams kyis ni bon nyid do::
23.3(1): phyin ci ma log yongs grub ni: bon nyid phyin ci ma log pa: rtogs pas rig pa'i 
23.4(1): ye shes te: kun btags skye bo'i spyod yul la: gzhan dbang g.yung drung sems 
23.5(1): dpa' yis: yongs su grub pa rdzogs sangs rgyas: mtshan nyid gang gis spyod yul 
23.6(1): na: yod pa mngon zhen kun btags pas: so sor skye bo'i shes pa 'khrul: mig 
23.7(1): nad can ltar spyod yul gyur: skye med bon rnams de bzhin gshegs: byis pa'i blo 
23.8(1): can mtshan 'dzin rnams: 'jig rten med pa'i bon la spyod: skye 'gag med pa'i 
23.9(1): skye med de: bon nyid de bzhin gshegs pa zhes: don ma rtogs pa'i byis blo can:
23.10(1): gzung 'dzin gnyis med bzhin yod pa: btags nas 'jig rten dag na med:
23.11(1): des na kun du btags pa de: shes pa 'khrul pa'i spyod yul gyur: gzhan dbang 
23.12(1): byang chub sems dpa' dag: 'jig rten pa yi spyod yul gyur: mig nad med cing 
23.13(1): bral ba yin: de ma mthong na de mi mthong : yongs grub bon nyid ma rtogs na:
23.14(1): gzung 'dzin gnyis bral mthong mi gtub: yongs grub bon nyid rtogs kyi rjes:
23.15(1): thob pa'i dag pa 'jig rten pa'i: ye shes kyi ni gzhan yang la: gzung 'dzin sgyu ma 
23.16(1): ltar rtogs te: sna tshogs snang yang dngos med dag: gzhan dbang rgyu rkyen las 
23.17(1): skyes pa: gnyis su 'dzin kyang yang dag med: yang dag yongs su grub pa ni:
23.18(1): sangs rgyas kyi ni spyod yul gyur: bon rnams mtshan nyid gsum la 'dus: med la 
23.19(1): yod btags kun du btags: rgyu rkyen skye ba gzhan gyis dbang : phyin ci log blos 
23.20(1): btags pa min: rgyu rkyen gyis kyang ma bskyed pa: thams cad yongs su grub tu 
23.21(1): 'dus: rang gi rnam par ma rig pa: mtshan nyid gsum yang der 'dus te: rang 
24.1(1): gi rig pa tsam la 'khrul: gzung 'dzin gnyis snang ma yin yul: log med kun 
24.2(1): btag kyang der 'dus: rang gi shes pa dngos por 'dzin: shes pa de nyid rgyu dang 
24.3(1): rkyen: gzhan gyis ma bskyed skye mi nus: gzhan dbang rnam par rig la 'dus:
24.4(1): rang gi rnam par rig tsam nyid: bon rnams thams cad snang ba yin: ngo bo ma 
24.5(1): skyes bon nyid yin: bon can bon nyid dbyer med pa: yongs grub kyi ni bon nyid 
24.6(1): kyang : rnam par rig tsam de la 'dus: de la mtshan nyid mtshan pa'i tshig: kun 
24.7(1): btags rang gi mtshan nyid ni: ci yang ma grub stong pas mtshon: gzhan dbang rgyu 
24.8(1): rkyen gzhan la rag: rang skye mi nus pa yis mtshon: yongs grub stong zhing bdag 
24.9(1): med mtshon: mtshon pa'i mtshan nyid kyang ma grub: kun btags 'khor ba'i sems 
24.10(1): can rnams: gzhan dbang de bzhin gshegs ngor grol: yongs grub bon nyid byang 
24.11(1): chub sems: gnas pa bya ba'i phyir du ni: med la mos pa rnams la ni: de bzhin 
24.12(1): kun btags med pa bstan: yod la mos pa gzhan dbang can: rang sems snang 
24.13(1): ba mi spang ste: btags la mos pa yongs grub bstan: kun btags log pa 
24.14(1): btags pa tsam: gzhan dbang snang spyod rnam par dag: yongs su grub pa'i bon 
24.15(1): nyid kyang : mi 'gyur gsum gyi mtshan nyid ldem: yon tan phyogs res gzugs 
24.16(1): dang bon: longs spyod rigs kyi dregs pa dang : mi yi gnyen po lha'i yon tan:
24.17(1): bon gyi dregs pa la sogs pa: zil gyis gnon pas drang ba'i phyir: gnyen po 
24.18(1): dregs pa zhi ba'i ched: gsang sngags zab cing khyad par du: gyur pa'i yon tan 
24.19(1): rnams brjod de: mos pa bskyed pa ka dag bstan: de dag dregs pa zhi ba'i 
24.20(1): gsang ba sngags kyi sgo ru gzhug: 'du shes log sred can rnams la: gsang sngags 
24.21(1): la mos ring brgyud can: rdul shugs dag la dga' ba la: gsang dang sbas pa'i 
25.1(1): gcus tshig brda: sbyor sgrol gnyis spyad grol skad sogs: sna tshogs zab mo'i don 
25.2(1): la gzhug: thar pa thob thabs 'du shes bsgyur: sngags don nyams su myong bar bya:
25.3(1): sha chen lnga dang bdud rtsi lnga: rnam par rtog pa kun sbyangs nas: rigs lnga sangs 
25.4(1): rgyas 'grub pa'i phyir: dam rdzas bdud rtsi longs spyod dam: rdzas lnga rigs lnga 
25.5(1): sangs rgyas na: rigs lnga ye shes ngo bo gnas: gdul bya rigs rgyud can la gnyis:
25.6(1): lha srin rigs dang mi rigs gnyis: lha srin rigs rgyud mtshan nyid zhugs: mi yi 
25.7(1): rigs rgyud ldem dgongs dang : lha srin dam rdzas ldem dgongs dang : ston pa skur 
25.8(1): bstan ldem dgongs sbyor: lha srin theg pa zhugs pa la: gti mug can ni tshangs pa 
25.9(1): klu: zhe sdang can ni gnod sbyin rigs: 'dod chags can ni ma mo sogs: dge 
25.10(1): bcu zhugs pa lha mi gnyis: theg pa rgyu zhugs nyan rang byang : 'bras bu zhugs pa 
25.11(1): de dag rnams: btul nas gsang sngags zab mo nyid: bde chen kun tu gcig pa 
25.12(1): yi: lta dgongs zab mo la zhugs pas: longs sku rigs lnga yab yum la: 'khor 
25.13(1): 'das gnyis kyi bde ba 'dus: 'khor ba'i bde bas mchod pa 'bul: 'das pa'i 
25.14(1): bde ba rigs lnga grub: yul med nam mkha'i rgyu rkyen gyis: rten dang bral ba'i rig 
25.15(1): pa 'gro: don dam bon nyid nam mkha' la: rig pa brten med du 'gro ba: mkha' 
25.16(1): 'gro rnams kyi tshogs kyi rje: sprul pa'i sku bstan drag po'i lha: sbyor dang sgrol ba'i 
25.17(1): las brtson pa: sku gsung thugs yon lha bzhi bstan: sku nyid khro gtum rab bstan 
25.18(1): kyang : tshad med byams pa khyab par snang : lta ba log pa lta ba bcoms: bu gcig 
25.19(1): ma ltar byams pa'i: gsod byed snying rje'i rang bzhin te: lta log 'khor ba'i rgya 
25.20(1): mtsho nas: mi grol bsgral nas bde la bkod: tshad med skyong ba snying rje ste: bsgral 
25.21(1): zhing bstab pa dga' ba'i mchog: lta ngan las grol sangs rgyas zhing : bsgral 
26.1(1): bstab tshad med dga' ba'i thabs: gdul bya yal ba mi dor btang : snyoms pa 
26.2(1): tshad med btang snyoms mod: thabs kyis gdul bya drang ba'i phyir: ma ltar byams 
26.3(1): dang sring ltar gdung : kun la byams pas zhing la spyad: sdang ba'i dgra dang gnod 
26.4(1): pa'i bgegs: snying rje drag pos gsod par bya: mtshan ldan rdzas mchog nyams 
26.5(1): med phyir: de ni dga' bas ma byin blang : brgyud pa'i tshig dang 'dra ba kun: rdzun 
26.6(1): smra btang snyoms chen po spyod: log sred can rnams bkrid drang ste: 'khor 'das 
26.7(1): kun la khyab pa gnas: bde chen mchog gi dngos grub thob: kun khyab zab mo sku 
26.8(1): gsum rdzogs: yum gyi ba gar zhugs pa ni: gsang ba sku ste rnal 'byor pa: yum 
26.9(1): la thig le zin pa'i dus: thig le gsang gnas gtsug tu zlog: gtsug gtor 
26.10(1): g.yas 'khyil gzugs su grub: dung zlum brtsegs pa'i gzhal med khang : gtsug 
26.11(1): gtor 'khor lo bsgyur rgyal por: rang lus rang dbang thob pa'i dus: 'dod pa'i 
26.12(1): yon tan lnga dang ldan: ji ltar spyod cing rol pa ni: tshogs kyi 'khor lo rol pa ste:
26.13(1): dbang yul gzugs sgra dri ro reg: rigs lnga sangs rgyas nyid la 'bul: dngos 
26.14(1): grub ji ltar 'dod pa'i don: gsol ba gdab cing mchod pas mchod: bdag 
26.15(1): dang lha gnyis dbyer med rol: 'jig rten bud med sbyor ba ni: phyi yi yan lag 
26.16(1): bzhi 'khyud dang : nang sbyor rlung sa me chu'i drang : gsang ba rtsa 'khor bzhi nas 
26.17(1): bskul: de kho na yi sbyor ba la: dkar dmar pad rdor nang 'phrad dus: ngos 
26.18(1): bzung sku yi sbyor ba'o:: bde bas tshims nas nyi zla gza': thugs kyi sbyor ba 
26.19(1): gsang dbang len: bla ma'i sbyin pa gsang ba'i dbang : rang gis rol bza' shes 
26.20(1): rab dbang : yid kyi bza' ba bde chen dbang : thun mong tshe yi rig 'dzin thob:
26.21(1): mchog gi g.yung drung lta bu'i sku: mngon du thob par nyid du bstan: gsung gi sbyor 
27.1(1): ba thig le de: gsang ba'i rtse nas gyen zlog cing : sbubs su nub cing lte bar zlog:
27.2(1): sgong ltar 'phrad cing snying khar zlog: seng ltar mgrin pa'i lce zhabs zlog: gsung ni 
27.3(1): tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan: gdul bya zhen chags can rnams la: 'dul byed 
27.4(1): gsang ba'i skus 'dul thabs: rang rkyen rang lus sku gsum rtogs: lus ngag 
27.5(1): yid la gang gnas pa: rtogs pa de ni longs sku ste: longs sku rgyan gyis brjid pa 
27.6(1): ltar: lus rang ngang gis brjid pa'o:: ngag ni sprul pa'i sku yin te: sprul sku

27.9(1): gzhi rnam par shes pa ni: kun gzhi bon sku gtan la dbab: rang bzhin dmigs

27.11(1): ba'i gzhi: rnam byang myang 'das gyis ni brten: dmigs pa rgya ma chad pa de: yul 
27.12(1): ni bon nyid lta ba ste: 'khor ni sgo lnga'i rnam par shes: nges tshig dkar nag bag 
27.13(1): chags gzhi: rtsal ni rnam shes lnga ldang ba: de ltar gnas 'gyur bon gyi sku: ye 
27.14(1): nas bon dbyings ye shes dang : me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi: yongs grub yang dag 
27.15(1): bon sku de: sku dang ye shes gang gis bsdus: ngo bo las dang gnas 'gyur ro:: ngo

27.18(1): bon sgo thams cad yangs par 'byed: de nyid gnas su 'gyur ba'i thabs: kun

28.1(1): snang ba: sems kyi rtog pa cir byung yang : de dag gang la nyam mi nga : yang dog 
28.2(1): med cing ma chags pa: kun gzhi me long lta bu yis: ye shes ngo bor gsal ba'o::
28.3(1): de yi las ni kun gzhi la: ma bslang ye shes mthong ba'i dus: phyi nang bon kun 
28.4(1): gzhi ltar snang : kun gzhi snang ba rang 'gyur dus: bon kun snang ba gsal ba'o::
28.5(1): bon rnams bon dbyings ye shes su: gnas 'gyur dus ni ma bcos pa: me long ye 
28.6(1): shes ma 'gags gsal: bon dbyings gsal la mi g.yo ba: gnas 'gyur dbyings 
28.7(1): shes 'du 'bral med: yang dag bon sku dri ma med: de ni dbyings shes bon gyi sku:
28.8(1): ye shes sku ni phung por grol: 'khor 'das longs spyod rgyan rdzogs pa: sor rtogs 
28.9(1): mnyam nyid gnyis la 'dus: longs sku ye shes gang gis bsdus: tshul khrims ting 
28.10(1): 'dzin phung po la: sku gnyis ye shes ngo bo dang : las dang gnas 'gyur ngo bo ni:
28.11(1): kun la 'jug cing gcod pa yid: bdag gis gzhan 'dzin nyon mongs can: las 
28.12(1): ni shes rab rnam grol sku: ye shes mthong ba'i phung po lnga: 'khor ba'i bde ba 'dod 
28.13(1): yon lnga: bud med longs spyod myang 'das kyi: bag chags sna tshogs so sor gcod:
28.14(1): nyon mongs can gyi yid kyi las: kun gzhi mthong du mi ster sgrib: gnas 'gyur 
28.15(1): kun gzhi bde stobs dang : mi 'jig pa las spyod pa na: rgyal srid btsun mo 'khor 
28.16(1): bcas so:: kun gzhi mkha' ltar snang ba'i dus: mtshan ma sna tshogs ma skyes rig:
28.17(1): bon rnams re dogs med par rtogs: yid ni sor rtogs ye shes 'gyur: kun 
28.18(1): gzhi mkha' ltar snang ba'i dus: rang bzhin 'dzin pa med pas na: don ni so sor 
28.19(1): tha mi dad: nyon mongs can gyi yid de ni: mnyam nyid ye shes gnas su 'gyur: ye 
28.20(1): shes gnyis 'dus longs sku'o:: gdul dka' sems can 'gro ba'i don: sprul pa'i 
28.21(1): 'khor lo chen po yang : zhi ba khro bo rang snang ba: sprul sku bya ba grub pa yi: bon 
29.1(1): dbyings mkha' dag pho brang na: longs sku rigs lnga'i sprul pa ste: gdul bya rigs 
29.2(1): drug sems can rnams: 'dul byed gshen drug 'gro don mdzad: ru tra la sogs 
29.3(1): gdug pa can:'dul ba khro bo'i sku rnams sprul: zhi khro gnyis kyi 'gro don mdzad:
29.4(1): ye shes ngo bo las ni 'gyur: ye shes gang gi bsdus na ni: bya ba grub pa'i ye shes te:
29.5(1): ngo bo dbang yul so sor 'dzin: sgo lnga las ni gzugs sogs mthong : gnas 
29.6(1): 'gyur kun gzhi mkha' ltar dus: yul gyi cir snang sems kyis rtogs: rang byung 
29.7(1): sems kyi mtshan nyid du: rig na sgo lnga'i rnam shes dpe: nan tan ye shes gnas su 
29.8(1): 'gyur: sprul pa sku yi 'dul ba bzhi: mngon sum 'dul dang thugs kyis 'dul:
29.9(1): rdzu 'phrul gyis 'dul rig pas 'dul: sna tshogs bsod nams 'dul ba sogs: sku 
29.10(1): gsung thugs nyid bsam mi khyab: don du mdzad pa brjod pa bral: zab mo sku 
29.11(1): gsum rdzogs pa la: sku dang ye shes snang ba dang : ye shes lnga yul gcig tu bsdu 
29.12(1): ba dang : yon tan ci ltar rnam grangs ni: ye shes lnga la don gsum ste: yul dang

48.11(1): dang 'gro: mtha' dang yul bral don dam pa: rnam grangs ma yin sangs rgyas 
48.12(1): thugs: rnam grangs thugs kyi mkhyen gzigs yul: stong pa bco brgyad rab tu dbye:
48.13(1): nang gi bon ni dbang po lnga: ther gzugs ma yin don dam pa: mig yor dngos 
48.14(1): med nang stong pa: phyi yi bon ni gzugs sgra sogs: 'jig 'gyur dngos med phyi 
48.15(1): stong pa: phyi nang skye mched gzung 'dzin med: yul dang yul bral phyi nang stong :
48.16(1): bon rnams ngo bo rang bzhin stong : gzhan stong med pa stong pa nyid: 'jig rten 
48.17(1): phyogs bcur chen po stong : myang 'das don dam dngos med stong : 'dus byas skye 
48.18(1): gnas 'gag bral stong : 'dus ma byas ni mkha' 'gog stong : rtag chad yod med 
48.19(1): mtha' 'das stong : 'khor ba thog mtha' med pas stong : bon rnams dor ba med 
48.20(1): pas stong : gang gi ma mdzad rang bzhin stong : phung khams skye mched bon rnams 
48.21(1): stong : gzugs sogs rang gi mtshan nyid stong : dus gsum gtogs rnams mi 
49.1(1): dmigs stong : dngos po dngos gzugs med pa stong : bon rnams rten 'brel ngo 
49.2(1): bo stong : dngos med ngo nyid stong pa nyid: rnam grangs don dam bco brgyad la:
49.3(1): rnam grangs ma yin don dam pa: spros pa'i mtha' brgyad bral ba yin: stong pa re 
49.4(1): la'ang mtha' brgyad khyab: de ni khyad par shes par bya: snod bcud snang ba bon 
49.5(1): can la: yang dag don dam med pa na: stong pa gtan phab nam mkha' bzhin:
49.6(1): mkha' la 'byung snang mi snang stong : 'khor 'das nam mkha' ngang stong gnas: de 
49.7(1): ltar kun rdzob don dam mo:: ngo bo gnas shing brten 'os pas: so so'i skye bo'i 
49.8(1): mos spyod gsum: mos spyod sa ni zhes pa la: bskal pa grangs med gcig gi bar:
49.9(1): g.yung drung sems dpa'i bon gyi dbyings: mos pa bsgom ste da dung yang : sangs 
49.10(1): rgyas ma mthong mos spyod bya: smon pa byams sems mngon du byas: bon la mos pa 
49.11(1): byed pa'o:: tshogs lam sgo gsum gyis bsogs pa: sbyor lam bon can mtshan med 
49.12(1): sbyor: g.yung drung sems dpa'i sa bcu la: 'jig rten las 'das byang chub nyid:
49.13(1): sems can don sgrub mthong bas na: rab tu dga' bar dga' ba sgoms: sbyin 
49.14(1): pa'i pha rol phyin dang sbyor: ltung ba'i cha phra kun kyang byang : 'chal ba'i tshul khrims 
49.15(1): dri ma med: tshul khrims pha rol phyin pa bya: nyan thos rang rgyal las 'das pa'i:
49.16(1): ting 'dzin phung po yongs su dag: ye shes snang ba chen po thob: 'od byed bzod pa 
49.17(1): phar phyin sbyor: nyon shes sgrib pa gnyis bsregs pa: byang chub phyogs kyi me 'od 
49.18(1): 'phro: brtson 'grus pha rol phyin dang sbyor: 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi bsgom zhing :
49.19(1): 'khor 'das gnyis ka mi gnas pa'i: shes rab yongs su dag bya ba: sbyang zhing 
49.20(1): bsgom pa shin tu dka': sgrub dka' shin tu sbyang dka' ba: bsam gtan pha rol 
49.21(1): phyin dang sbyor: 'khor 'das gnyis la mi gnas shing : mtshan med ngang 'jug ye 
50.1(1): shes la: gnas shing gzigs pas mngon du gyur: shes rab pha rol phyin dang sbyor:
50.2(1): mtshan ma med la bgrod pa gcig: nye zhing ring du song bar gyur: thabs kyi pha rol 
50.3(1): phyin dang sbyor: mtshan ma yod med kyis rtsol ba'i: 'du shes bskyed nus mi g.yo ba:
50.4(1): smon lam pha rol phyin dang sbyor: so sor yang dag rig pa'i bon: ting 'dzin nam 
50.5(1): mkha' sprin bzhin khyab: ye shes pha rol phyin dang sbyor: de ltar phar phyin bcu ldan 
50.6(1): pas: dang po ser sna mi ldan pas: sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: gnyis pa 
50.7(1): 'chal pa mi gnas pas: tshul khrims pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: gsum pa khong khro mi 
50.8(1): gnas pas: bzod pa'i pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: bzhi pa le lo mi gnas pas:
50.9(1): brtson 'grus pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: lnga pa rnam g.yeng mi gnas pas: bsam 
50.10(1): gtan pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: drug pa gti mug mi gnas pas: shes rab pha rol 
50.11(1): phyin pa rdzogs: bdun pa thabs la mi mkhas bor: thabs kyi pha rol phyin pa rdzogs:
50.12(1): brgyad pa gud smon mi 'debs pas: smon lam pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: dgu pa nyan 
50.13(1): rang sar mi ltung : stobs kyi pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: bcu pa ye gnas don rtogs 
50.14(1): pas: ye shes pha rol phyin pa rdzogs: mos pa spyod pa'i sa nas drod: dang po rnam 
50.15(1): par byang ba la: dkar po mthong ba zhes bya ba: bon dang gang zag bdag med 
50.16(1): bzod: byang chub rigs ldan rigs kyi sa: dgra bcoms 'bras thob dang po nas:
50.17(1): yas bgrangs grags zhugs brgyad pa'i sa: rgyun zhugs 'bras bu de kho na: rtag pa 
50.18(1): mthong ba mthong ba'i sa: lan gcig phyir 'ong 'dod khams kyi: 'dod chags srab 
50.19(1): byas bstabs pa'i sa: phyir mi 'ong la gnas 'dun sa: gnod spong 'dod chags 
50.20(1): bral ba'i sa: bsrung ba'i rang bzhin sngar byas grub: don mi nyams phyir bsrung 
50.21(1): ba'i sa: dngos su dgra bcom pa yi sa'o:: nyan thos sa bdun rnam par gnas:
51.1(1): chu rgyun lta bu rgyun du zhugs: tshe 'di mya ngan mi 'da' ba'i: lan gcig 'jig rten 
51.2(1): skye phyi'o:: tha ma'i bon ni lnga spangs pas: 'dod khams mi skye phyir mi 'ong : las 
51.3(1): nyon gyi dgras myang 'das kyi: bar gcod rnams bcoms dgra bcom mo:: theg pa 
51.4(1): chen po'i sa gsum la: kun tu 'dus ni dbyings ye shes: gnyis med 'bras bu 
51.5(1): bon gyi sku: pad+ma can ni bon sku'i las: gzugs sku mi 'gag longs sku'o:: yi ge 
51.6(1): 'khor lo dpa' bo lnga: gdul bya gang mos sprul sku 'byung : de bzhin gshegs pa'i 
51.7(1): sa zhes bya'o:: byang chub phyogs kyi lam gsum por: tshogs lam mthong lam sbyor 
51.8(1): ba'i lam: phyogs gyur sum cu rtsa bdun te: dran pa nye bar bzhag pa la: lus 
51.9(1): sems tshor ba bon dang bzhi: rang mtshan shes rab kyis brtag ste: don rnams 
51.10(1): dran pa shas che ba: tshogs lam lus dran tshor ba dran: lus ni mi rtag sdug bsngal 
51.11(1): dang : bdag med tshor bas bde dang sdug: btang snyoms bar la nye bar bzhag:
51.12(1): sems dran bon ni dran pa ste: nyer bzhag tshogs brgyad don rtsol ba: bon dran 
51.13(1): kun nyon rnam byang don: tshogs lam chung ngu nyer bzhag ste: yang dag pa ni spong 
51.14(1): byed pa: mi dge ma byas mi byed spong : dge ba ma byas byed pa spel: tshogs kyi lam 
51.15(1): ni 'bring po ste: sdig pa mi dge thams cad spong : sgo gsum ma skyes phyis mi bskyed:
51.16(1): mi dge sngar skyes zhen thag spong : sgo gsum dge ba ma skyes bskyed: skyes pa rnams 
51.17(1): kyang gong du spel: rdzu 'phrul gyis ni rkang pa bzhi: 'dun pa dang ni brtson 'grus 
51.18(1): dang : sems dang spyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin: mkha' la 'gro sogs rdzu 'phrul gyis:
51.19(1): 'dun pa'i 'dun pa drag po bskyed: brtson 'grus kyis ni myur du sgrub: sems pa 
51.20(1): yas ni gang 'dod sgrub: spyod pa 'bras bu gang yin spyod: sgo gsum tshogs lam 
51.21(1): chen po sbyor: sbyor lam dbang lnga stobs lnga te: dad pa brtson 'grus dran pa dang :
52.1(1): ting 'dzin shes rab 'di lnga'i dbang : sems las rang gyur rgyu la ni: thar pa cha 
52.2(1): mthun dge ba bskyed: dad pa'i dbang pos dad pa dbang : dran pas dran pa ting 
52.3(1): 'dzin 'dzin: shes rab shes rab dbang thob pa: stobs lnga dad dang dran pa dang :
52.4(1): brtson 'grus ting 'dzin shes rab lngas: ma dad brjed ngas le lo dang : g.yeng ba 
52.5(1): shes bzhin ma yin pa: mi mthun phyogs gyur lnga po yis: bar chad mi nus dad pa 
52.6(1): sogs: gnyen po mthus bskyed stobs lnga pos: drod rtse bzod mchog mthong lam 
52.7(1): sbyor: bzung ba rang bzhin med na drod: 'phags lam rtsa yi rtse mo rtse: 'dzin pa 
52.8(1): rang bzhin med pas bzod: yid ches 'jig rten bon mchog bzhi: nyon mongs 
52.9(1): bsregs pas me 'dra'i drod: dge snga mi brten g.yo ba'i rtse: bden pa rab dang 
52.10(1): ldan pa bzod: yul gyur 'jig rten bon gyi mchog: sgom lam byang chub yan lag 
52.11(1): bdun: dran dang bon rnams 'byed pa dang : brtson 'grus dang ni dga' ba dang :
52.12(1): shin tu sbyang dang ting 'dzin dang : btang snyoms mthong lam de kho na: byang chub rgyu 
52.13(1): gyur yan lag bdun: sgrub pa'i rgyu yin bsgom pa'i las: dran pa yang dag 
52.14(1): dmigs mi brjod: bon rnams ji lta ji snyed 'byed: brtson 'grus 'khor ba las 
52.15(1): 'das byed: dga' bas sgo gsum phan 'dogs pa: shin tu sbyangs bas sems 
52.16(1): las rung : ting 'dzin sems ni rtse gcig pa: btang snyoms yan lag 'du byed 
52.17(1): gnyen: bon nyid don la yang yang bsgom: dang po sa gnas rab tu dga':
52.18(1): mthong ba'i 'phags lam yan lag brgyad: yang dag lta ba rtogs pa dang : ngag 
52.19(1): dang las mtha' 'tsho ba dang : rtsol ba dran pa ting nge 'dzin: lta bas mthong lam 
52.20(1): mngon du byas: rtog pas mi rtog par mi smra: ngag gis col ces 'dul bon ston:
52.21(1): lus kyis mtha' bya gzhan mi byed: 'tsho bas yo byad gang rung 'gyur: rtsol bas lta 
53.1(1): ba zin pa rtsol: dran pas zhi gnas bying rgod med: ting 'dzin bsam gtan 
53.2(1): mngon du 'byung : ma mthong don mthong mthong ba'i lam: sa ni gnyis nas brgyad 
53.3(1): pa'i bar: rang gzhan don gnyis sa lam sbyar: mos spyod sa nas dang po'i bar:
53.4(1): rang don sgrub pa kho na la: nyon mongs 'khor ba'i 'dam la gnas: gdul bya de 
53.5(1): gnas don mi nus: sa ni gnyis nas brgyad pa'i bar: rang gzhan gnyis ka'i 
53.6(1): don byed de: bag nyal ma bral rang don dang : nyon mongs rgyu 'bras gzhan don 
53.7(1): mdzad: mthar phyin lam ni sa dgu bcu: rang gzhan don gnyis mtha' ru phyin:
53.8(1): g.yung drung lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin: bon rnams nam mkha'i dkyil lta bu: rtogs 
53.9(1): pa'i ngang gnas bar mi chod: de dus nyon mngos dug las grol: nyan thos byang 
53.10(1): sems mi slob ste: slob pa'i lam bsdams mi slob lam: de'i tshe de ltar ting 'dzin 
53.11(1): gyis: bon rnams mkha' dkyil ltar rtogs pas: 'bras bu bon sku thob par byed:
53.12(1): thog med gnas pas khyad par lam: de ltar mtshan nyid rgyu yi theg: gsum gyi shes 
53.13(1): rab blo khar dbyer: bya rgyud dag pa bon nyid dang : ye shes mtha' bzhi dang bral 
53.14(1): ba: gzhan don sa bon snying rje dang : tshogs bsags yan lag bdun dag bya:
53.15(1): tshad med bzhi dang byang sems bskyed: stong nyid sgra sngags yig 'bru thugs: ye 
53.16(1): shes rdzogs pa'i lha sku bsgom: srung ba'i zhal phyir bstan nas srung : rje bran lta bu'i 
53.17(1): spyan drangs mchod: dus bzang gtsang sbra dka' thub spyod: mi tshe bdun nas 
53.18(1): sangs rgyas so:: rigs kyi lha mi 'gro ba 'dul: gnyis ka'i rgyud ni 'thug po bkod:
53.19(1): rigs bzhi sku gnas rdul shugs spyod: dka' thub g.yeng ba btul sgom zhugs:
53.20(1): ye shes 'og min dbyings su blta: spro bsdus bsgom pa'i lha sku gsal: ting 'dzin 
53.21(1): byin rlabs dbang bskur mchod: rnam par mi rtog mngon byang sku: rnam snang 
54.1(1): rigs lnga yab yum bskor: bdag dang lha gnyis spun grogs blta: bstod pa 
54.2(1): bsod nams ldan phyir bya: mi tshe drug nas 'thug po bkod: rnam snang zhabs drung 
54.3(1): sangs rgyas so:: de ltar tshe lo brgya pa'i dus: ye gshen chen po rgyud la gsum:
54.4(1): rgyud lung man ngag gsum du bstan: rgyud la rgyan bdun bshad dgos pa: dang po 
54.5(1): gleng slong grangs lnga dang : gnyis pa rdzogs sangs rgyas pa'i tshul: gsum pa rgyas 
54.6(1): bshad mtha' drug dang : bzhi pa tshul bzhin bshad pa'i tshul: lnga pa bshad thabs 
54.7(1): dbye ba gnyis: drug pa gang zag snod dbye ba: bdun pa bden pa'i dgongs par 
54.8(1): shes: gleng slong grangs ni dri ba lnga: dang po rgyud 'di'i ming ni ci: rten gyi gang zag 
54.9(1): gang gi don: ston pa'i bdag nyid su zhig gis: rgyud 'di'i ldang tshad ji lta bu:
54.10(1): dgos pa ci zhig yod pa shes: dang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyis: dgongs pa'i 
54.11(1): bskyed rim gtso bor bstan: a dkar theg pa rgyud 'di'i ming : skye bo 'dod 
54.12(1): chags can la sogs: nyon mongs dug lnga 'dul slad du: ston pa kun bzang 
54.13(1): rigs lngas gsungs: cho ga rgyud kyi ldang tshad ni: dbang dang dkyil 'khor phrin 
54.14(1): las bzhi: dgos pa mchog thun dngos grub sgrub: gnyis pa sangs rgyas tshul la 
54.15(1): bzhi: rgyud dang gleng gzhi nges tshig rgyud: chags can chags bral sangs rgyas tshul:
54.16(1): rgyud mi'i las kyi sangs rgyas so:: gleng gzhi rab tu sangs rgyas so:: nges tshig 
54.17(1): 'dul ba'i sdom pa blang : rgyu ni 'bras bu sangs rgyas 'dod: gsang ba sngags la 
54.18(1): bshad tshul gnyis: sngags la mtshan nyid gnyis 'byed pa: 'chags pa bcas pa'i 
54.19(1): sangs rgyas tshul: rgyud lha lus rigs lnga sangs rgyas: gleng gzhi rigs lnga gcig tu 
54.20(1): gyur: nges tshig g.yung drung la sogs bzhugs: rgyu ni sgegs pa la sogs spyod:
54.21(1): 'di ltar sngags kyi sangs rgyas so:: gsum pa rgyas bshad mtha' drug la: don gyi 
55.1(1): mtha' brtan drang don gnyis: tshig mtha' dgongs bshad dgongs min gnyis:
55.2(1): tshig don gnyis ka'i mtha' brten pa: sgra ni ji bzhin ji bzhin min: skal ngan 
55.3(1): sbas te bshad drang don: thun mong dngos grub thob 'dod cing : mtshan ma la 
55.4(1): dga' bskyed rim ste: yang dag don bstan nges pa'i don: dgos pa dngos grub 
55.5(1): mchog 'grub cing : lam nye 'dod rdzogs rim pa ston: bzhi pa tshul bzhin bshad 
55.6(1): pa la: sgra tshig sbas dang mthar thug yin: lnga pa bshad thabs dbye ba gnyis: sgra 
55.7(1): ni ji bzhin dgos yin dang : drang don yig don spyi don bshad: ji bzhin ma yin 
55.8(1): nges pa'i don: dgongs bshad sbas pa mthar thug bshad: rang dbang ma bskur 
55.9(1): tshogs pa la: rang gi dbang bskur slob ma 'dod: drug pa snod kyi dbye ba la: u 
55.10(1): dpal pad+ma dkar dmar dang : tsan dan rin po che yi dpal: bskyed rim sgyu lus 
55.11(1): kun rdzob bden: rdzogs rim 'od gsal don dam pa: a dkar sngags kyi rgyud 
55.12(1): don bstan: ye gshen lung gi bcud 'byin pa: theg chen sgrub pa'i yang snying che:
55.13(1): dus gsum sangs rgyas kun gyi lam: sgrub chen lung bdun gnyis gcig ston: snang 
55.14(1): srid ye sangs lta ba'i lugs: lha sku phyag rgya bskyed rim lugs: bzlas brjod 
55.15(1): bsnyen pa sngags kyi lugs: bon nyid yul rol sbyor ba'i lugs: zhing bcu rtsad 
55.16(1): gcod bsgral ba'i lugs: tshogs kyi 'khor lo mchod pa'i lugs: dbang bskur

55.21(1): ma blo 'byed zab mo bshad: ye gshen rdzogs pa 'gyur med pa: ye gnas bon nyid 
56.1(1): mkha' ltar bu: phyi snod nang bcud rnam par dag: lta ba'i dkyil 'khor mkha' 
56.2(1): lding 'dra: sems nyid nang nas rang gsal te: rgya mtsho ma bskyod ltar gnas pa:
56.3(1): sgo gsum rnam rtog zil gyis gnon: seng skad gcan zan sgra bzhin du: rtogs 
56.4(1): dus 'bras bu 'byung ba ste: yid bzhin rin chen lta bu la: rtogs ni mi 'gyur khu 
56.5(1): byug ltar: snang srid thams cad ye sangs rgyas: 'bras bu bon sku kho nar 'dod:
56.6(1): bla med theg chen rgyal sa zin: rgyal rigs bla tshe rta ru rgyu: rang gi rgyal srid skyong 
56.7(1): bar byed: rje rigs bla tshe lug rgyu 'byung : sgo gsum spyod dal chu rgyun ltar: bram 
56.8(1): ze'u rigs ni bla tshe ra: me 'dra rno sreg rab tu 'bar: dmangs rigs bla tshe sha ba 
56.9(1): 'byung : rlung dang 'dra ste mi sdod 'gro: gdol rigs bla tshe phag tu rgyug: gdol pa 
56.10(1): sgo gsum khro gtum che: mi rigs de rnams sngon gyi las: 'phral skal gang ldan 
56.11(1): brtag par bya: rgyal rigs rje rigs bram ze'u rigs: rang bzhin ngang gi tshul 
56.12(1): gshis bzang : ngan pa'i las dang spyod pa spong : ras snam dkar po sor tshur 
56.13(1): len: gshis kyi dkar nag yon tan la: tshos kyi bsgyur gtub nus mi nus: blo 
56.14(1): sbyong man ngag de ltar sbyor: dad pas srog lus longs spyod gtang : bla mar gus 
56.15(1): dang yi dam bsnyen: snod kyi skyon spong shes rab bskyed: tshig dang spyod pa dam tshig 
56.16(1): nges: zhing sa gshin la lo smin bzhin: slob ma gzhi legs man ngag smin: dngos 
56.17(1): grub rnam gnyis rgyud la thob: slob ma'i blo gang rnam pa brgyad: dang po'i slob ma 
56.18(1): dad cing smin: gnyis pa brtson 'grus grogs su che: gsum pa mos gus byin 
56.19(1): rlabs 'byung : bzhi pa gtang phod bka' drin len: lnga pa rgyud ldan rgol ba 
56.20(1): 'joms: drug pa rigs rgyud rgyal po ltar: bdun pa lta ngan zil gyis gnon:
56.21(1): brgyad pa sku gsum dgongs mthar phyin: de ltar ldan pas gdams ngag sbyin:
57.1(1): sgrub pa'i lung bdun bstan par bya: rgyud sbyin mtshan nyid drug ldan te: dang po bla 
57.2(1): ma byin rlabs nye: gnyis pa gdams zab rgyud grol gyur: gsum pa zab don blo 
57.3(1): tshod mkhas: bzhi pa dbang bskur sku gsum smin: lnga pa byin ldan nges shes 'char:
57.4(1): drug pa yang dag don ston nus: de ltar lung gi snod du bstan: blo zhan gsang 
57.5(1): sngags 'jug ma nus: shes rab chung bas don mi rtogs: ci ltar sgrub kyang 'grub 
57.6(1): mi 'gyur: phung bar byed dang gnyis ka sreg: bla ma mi bkur bsgrub mi nus: lta 
57.7(1): spyod mi nus pa la gsang : mi rtog pa shes gti mug gnyid: 'dod chags bde 
57.8(1): shes bud med bsten: zhe sdang gsang shes zhing bcu gsad: nga rgyal lam slong lta ba 
57.9(1): mtho: phrag dog lta ngan 'joms pa byed: dug lnga'i spyod pa rmad du byung : gsang 
57.10(1): sngags dngos grub rang la 'byung : bon nyid sems kyi bcos su med: sems nyid 
57.11(1): ye nas sangs rgyas yin: gzhan nas sangs rgyas tshol du med: lta spyod ma rtogs 
57.12(1): rtsol sgrub kyang : 'bras bu sku gsum dngos grub rnams: thob pa mi 'gyur bla ma 
57.13(1): nyid: tshogs gnyis gtso bor spyi bor bsgom: gdams ngag dran zhing rtogs pa 
57.14(1): shar: 'bras bu ye shes tshogs chen rdzogs: tshogs bsags phyi yi sgros 'dog gcod:
57.15(1): nang gi rang byung ye shes ston: gsang ba lhan skyes bon rnams grol: rnam dag bla 
57.16(1): ma dbang bskur nus: bla ma yon tan bdun ldan pa: gzhan du mi ltos yon tan
